</div>                            <div class="top10-section-list-text top10-content"><p><b>Your logo is the face of your brand, and it deserves love and attention. </b>While you could hire a professional agency to design yours for thousands of dollars, theres no guarantee youll be satisfied with the result.</p>
<p>Traditional design agencies are a relic of the past.<b> By commissioning your design to an online logo design platform, you can receive equally good designs  if not better  much quicker and for a fraction of the cost. </b>But with so many options, how will you know which platforms right for you? <b></b></p>
<p>Thats where I come in.. As a long-time graphic designer and part of the Website Planet team, I set out on a quest to find the best new logo for our site. <b>I spent months testing all the major logo design platforms to see where I could get the highest quality for the best price</b>. Services with intuitive interfaces, easy hiring processes, and excellent customer support earned extra points.</p>
<p>Only the best logo design services that met my strict standards made the shortlist. Look at the final designs below, consider each platforms strengths, and pick one that ticks all the right boxes for you. You can also jump down to <a href="#full_story">learn more about my methodology</a>.</p>

                                    <div class="top10-vendor-list-item-content top10-content"><p><em><strong>The logo we got from DesignCrowd won the office vote, and it is now our new logo for Website Planet!</strong></em>That is definitely an impressive achievement, and you might be wondering why DesignCrowd isnt ranked #1 on my list.</p>
<p>Well, we all like the logo I got from DesignCrowd, but I still had a couple of issues with the platform. First, there was the price. When you can hire a designer on Fiverr for as little as $5, it just doesn&#8217;t make sense to pay over $100 for DesignCrowd. My second issue was the user interface &#8211; I didnt like all the calls-to-action and other distractions on the site.</p>
<p>You can run logo design contests on DesignCrowd and receive multiple proposals and ideas from professional designers. That said, I chose to work one-on-one with a designer instead. <strong>With DesignCrowd&#8217;s cheapest package, I couldnt choose my own designer</strong>, but I did pay a little extra to hire one of the top designers &#8211; a wise investment. There&#8217;s also a 60-day money-back guarantee, so you don&#8217;t have to worry about being stuck with a design you don&#8217;t like.</p>

                                    <div class="top10-vendor-list-item-content top10-content"><p>99designs can be a bit pricey compared to the other services on this list, but it offers <strong>excellent value for your money</strong>, especially if you have long-term design work. <p>I decided to run a logo design contest to see what I would get. I received about 40 different submissions of varying quality; as youd expect, some werent usable. Still, I was able to narrow them down to <strong>a few options that I really liked.</strong> Then we had an office vote, and the chosen winner was my favorite as well. Communicating with the designer to ask for revisions was easy and I had no problem getting exactly what I wanted.</p>
<p>If you dont want your competitors to know what youre up to, you can run a <b>private design contest</b> <strong>with 99designs </strong>for an extra fee. Agencies can sign up for 99designs Pro, which includes expedited service and a dedicated account manager.</p>

                                    <div class="top10-vendor-list-item-content top10-content"><p>LogoMaker offers two options: you can use the online logo generator to <strong>design your own logo</strong> or work directly with a professional designer. All you have to do is fill out a quick brief, and a designer will be contact you to discuss your logo. It doesnt get much easier than this.</p>
<p>The DIY logo editor is easy to use, but it does feel clunky at times. <b>You can tell Logo Maker hasnt received any updates in a long time</b><b>.</b> Although the <b>customization options</b> are okay, the available design templates are extremely outdated. No matter how hard I tried, I couldnt get this tool to come up with something that didnt look like it time-traveled from the early 00s. Then again, the 00s are coming back in style&#8230;</p>
<p>LogoMaker definitely needs to make some improvements. That said, the company offers additional business services, such as domain names, websites, and a range of stationery and merchandise you can have your logo printed on.</p>
                                        <div class="top10-row top10-vendor-list-item-more">
                                            <p class="vendor-more-row">More on LogoMaker</p>                                            <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=175531&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VisitSiteLink_175531_top10_159_44&post_id=159&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=&amp=0" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VisitSiteLink_175531_top10_159_44', 'logomaker', this,  true  );"><b>Visit LogoMaker ></b>
                                            </a>
                                            <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/logo-design-services/logomaker/" class="top10-vendor-list-item-more-first-a" target="_blank">Read our LogoMaker review                                            </a>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </li>                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </section>            <section class="top10-section top10-section-desc">
                <div class="top10-container">
                    <div class="top10-row top10-content">                            <h2 class="top10-section-desc-title" id="top10-section-desc-title"><span id="full_story">How I Compared The Best and Worst Logo Maker Services Out There (Or, What I Did on My Summer Vacation)</a></h2>                        <div class="top10-section-descBlock"><p></p> Im kidding, of course. Im an adult, so I dont take vacations until the week between Christmas and New Years. But seriously, this project took me a few months, and it puts me in a unique position: I have personally tried more different logo design services than most people ever will. 
<p></p> Once I was just a guy whos been designing websites for over a decade, and writing about it, too. I am now a guy who has also sat around thinking, Does this shade of pink look professional enough for our logo? a <em>lot</em>. In all honesty, though, Ive never had an experience quite like it in all of my years as a designer. 
<p></p> <strong>Ive tested the limits of AI-based logo design and given a bunch of different designers more creative freedom than they actually knew what to do with. </strong>Tremble, Mortals, and pray that I put enough details in your design brief so you feel like you know what to do! And make the design pop more! 
<p></p> I do have to say that this whole process was pretty cool. I was given the task of testing a whole bunch of different logo makers and design services for two reasons: 
<ol>
<li><strong>To find out which ones are best, which ones are the worst, and write it all down for you. You know, the entire point of this site.</strong></li>
<li>The top brass at Website Planet called for a new logo, so this isnt just a collection of reviews; its a contest. The best logo wins, and will be the new logo here at Website Planet.</li>
</ol> Read on to see the winning logo. 
<p></p> I dove into this project with my eyes and heart wide open, ready to experience the best logos that you can get really fast, and on a budget. You wont find any 5,000 to 20,000 USD rebrands here; I did not have the time or the budget for that. <strong>These are logos you could get for as little as 5 USD (and one service is entirely free), and some might cost up to 400 USD.</strong> 
<p></p> If you need a good-looking logo thats not going to completely break the bank, I probably tested the right service for you. Its in here, somewhere. 
<h3>Methodologies</h3>
<p></p> All right, so how exactly did I test these services? That greatly depends, as each one is a little different, and some are a lot different. <strong>On the whole, these services fall into two main categories: DIY and DIFM. Thats Do It Yourself and Do It For Me.</strong> 
<p></p> Ah, theres a joke in there somewhere. Dont tell the kids. 
<h3>DIY (Do It Yourself)</h3>
<p></p> These are the services where you basically design your own logo with the tools provided. These tools usually include some sort of visual editor (a way to select your preferred icons, colors, and fonts, and change the layout), a big old library of icons and/or predesigned logo templates, and sometimes some artificial intelligence (henceforth referred to as AI for convenience). 
<p></p> <strong>I tested almost all of these services in pretty much the same way.</strong> I just followed the instructions on screen (and usually recorded this process on video), paid for the logo, and then wrote my review, evaluating the following main factors: 
<ol>
<li>The quality of the AI, if it was present.</li>
<li>The quality of the icon/logo library.</li>
<li>How advanced the logo editor was, and how easy it was to use.</li>
<li>The available image formats.</li>
<li>Add-ons, such as images scaled for social media, or personal attention from a real designer.</li>
<li>Extra services, such as printing and web design.</li>
<li>The sites ease of use overall.</li>
<li>The customer support offered by the service.</li>
<li>The pricing plans/packages.</li>
</ol> <strong>I contacted support three times for each service, trying out as many different support options as I could,</strong> including phone support, email support, ticket systems, and live chat. Thats right, I got out of my comfort zone and actually <em>talked</em> to people, and I did it all for you, dear readers. It was all for you. 
<h3>DIFM (Do It For Me)</h3>
<p></p> As the name implies, these are the services where you hire someone else to do <em>all</em> the heavy lifting. You tell the designers what you want, as clearly as you can manage, and they do their best to give it to you. Most of these services allow you to run a contest, or hire individual designers as you see fit. 
<p></p> <strong>In order to get the widest possible range of design examples, we ran contests whenever we had the option.</strong> We evaluated these services based on the following factors: 
<ol>
<li>How easy it was to run a contest.</li>
<li>The quality and quantity of designs submitted to our contests.</li>
<li>How easy it was to manage and organize submitted designs.</li>
<li>How easy it was to communicate with the designer/s you chose.</li>
<li>How long it takes to get your logo.</li>
<li>How easy it is to browse designer profiles and work history, in case you want to hire one individually.</li>
<li>Add-on services, such as having your contest featured by the site, or having a guaranteed number of top designers participating in your contest.</li>
<li>The other services offered by some of these community-based sites, like web design, print design, and more.</li>
<li>The personal support offered by the service.</li>
<li>The pricing plans/packages.</li>
</ol> Again, I made three support requests to each service, via as many different means as they offered. There was a lot more talking to other people in general when reviewing these services, so I hope you appreciate my dedication. (Please note: Im being a little hyperbolic with the whole Im asocial thing.) 
<h3>The Exceptions</h3>
<p></p> <strong>Two of the DIFM services I tested do not give you the option of running contests, and so I had to test them a little bit differently.</strong> 
<p></p> In <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/logo-design-services/fiverr-logo-design/" target="_blank" ><strong>Fiverr</strong></a>s case, you just browse for designers, pick the one you want to work with, and hope you picked the right one. In order to get a range of designs, we chose to work with three designers: one whose prices started at 5 USD, one whose prices started at 40 USD, and one whose prices started at 400 USD. The 400 dollar designer was verified and vetted by Fiverrs Pro program. 
<p></p> <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/logo-design-services/the-logo-company/" target="_blank" ><strong>The Logo Company</strong></a> operates more like a traditional design agency, but apparently has lots of designers. You provide your project brief, and someone chooses the designers most likely to suit your needs. You get five initial concepts and unlimited redraws/revisions for one single payment. Theres not a lot to say about the methodology here, other than that I followed their process, and got myself a logo. 
<h2 id="hselect-1">My Personal Experience with 10 Different Logo Services</h2>
<p></p> Heres the part where I try to condense an estimated 24,000 words (this is a rather haphazard estimate at best) into a list of ten logo design services, with a couple of paragraphs each. <strong>These are not all of the services I tested, nor will they be the last.</strong> If you dont see the one youre looking for, use the search bar at the top of this page. Theres a decent chance that youll find a full review. 
<p></p> Here goes, and may Sir Terry Pratchett (my favorite author) guide me. 
<h3>99designs (DIFM &#8211; Contest)</h3>
<p></p> <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/logo-design-services/99designs/" target="_blank" ><strong>99designs</strong></a> has been running contests for a long time, and theyve been refining their process all along. That refinement shows; of all the DIFM-type services on this list, this may well be the easiest one to use. 
<p></p> <strong>In about five days, I had over 40 design submissions to look through,</strong> and 99designs made organizing all of this quite easy. I had a little trouble deciding which logo I wanted, so I sent a poll around the office for feedback (theres built-in functionality for this). Communication with the designer was smooth, and overall I enjoyed my experience. 
<p></p> Here were some of the logos that made it to the semifinals: 
<figure id="attachment_1798390" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1798390"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:76.061776061776% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/experience3-semifinals.jpg"  width="1295" height="985" alt="experience3 semifinals" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/experience3-semifinals.jpg"   width="1295" height="985" alt="experience3 semifinals" class="border wp-image-1798390 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1798390"class="wp-caption-text">Let the voting begin to choose the next logo for Website Planet</figcaption></figure> The final logo was chosen for its colorful style, and overall aesthetic. Despite its minimalist simplicity, it just feels like it has a lot of personality, fits the overall theme of our website, and looks gorgeous. You cant ask for a lot more.<br />
<span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:33.246584255042% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/Website-Planet-e1642675535611.png"  width="1537" height="511" alt="Website Planet e1642675535611" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/Website-Planet-e1642675535611.png"   width="1537" height="511" alt="Website Planet e1642675535611" class="border aligncenter wp-image-1798421 size-full ll-img"/></span>

<h3>DesignCrowd (DIFM &#8211; Contest Sort Of Not Really)</h3>
<p></p> <strong>DesignCrowd has a large community with some great designers, but the user experience leaves something to be desired.</strong> There are far too many calls to action and general distractions from whatever task you want to complete at any given time. 
<p></p> We tried to start a contest, but what we started was a project, which turned out to be a catch-all term for both single-designer jobs and contests. And contests are more expensive. Basically, we hired one single designer by accident, and someone from DesignCrowd picked them out for us. Fortunately, we also paid extra for access to their top designers, so we got a good one. 
<p></p> Here are some of their concepts after one round of refinements: 
<figure id="attachment_1007874" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1007874"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:75.03751875938% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image25.jpg"  width="1999" height="1500" alt="Logos from DesignCrowd logo contest" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image25.jpg"   width="1999" height="1500" alt="Logos from DesignCrowd logo contest" class="border wp-image-1007874 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1007874"class="wp-caption-text">Design Crowd logo options</figcaption></figure> The final logo was one of several based on a websites and space theme that the designer provided us with. <strong>To their credit, this designer went above and beyond to provide lots of different options in a <em>very</em> short time frame.</strong> This logo fits our layout needs, existing color scheme, theme of the site, and even if it is a little cliche it looks good. 
<span class="ll-smallimg-wrapper " style="max-width: 570px"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:28.070175438596% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image13.png"  width="570" height="160" alt="Website Planet logo from DesignCrowd" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image13.png"   width="570" height="160" alt="Website Planet logo from DesignCrowd" class="border aligncenter wp-image-1008079 ll-img"/></span></span>

<h3>DesignEvo (DIY)</h3>
<p></p> DesignEvo has a big library of premade logos and no AI, so they dont ask you a lot of questions about what sort of logo you want. Some of these logos are quite good, and some look like theyre from the 90s. Aside from the premade logos, though, theres also another large library of more basic icons and shapes so you can build your own logo design with their logo editor. 
<figure id="attachment_1798451" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1798451"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:49.895833333333% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/templates.jpg"  width="1920" height="958" alt="templates" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/templates.jpg"   width="1920" height="958" alt="templates" class="border wp-image-1798451 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1798451"class="wp-caption-text">Examples of DesignEvos logo templates</figcaption></figure> And what an editor it is!<strong> Its the most flexible, most useful app in this space Ive encountered so far.</strong> Its not a full image editor, of course, but if you put the time in, you can absolutely create a unique-looking logo. 
<figure id="attachment_1798482" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1798482"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:78.97233201581% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/library.jpg"  width="1265" height="999" alt="library" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/library.jpg"   width="1265" height="999" alt="library" class="border wp-image-1798482 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1798482"class="wp-caption-text">Using the Design Evo editor to create a logo</figcaption></figure> The one I made could be a lot more unique-looking, Ill admit. But hey, I had limited time, and wanted to show off the quality of their premade logos and icons in any case. 
<span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:28.473804100228% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/logo-28.png"  width="1756" height="500" alt="logo 28" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/logo-28.png"   width="1756" height="500" alt="logo 28" class="border aligncenter wp-image-1798511 size-full ll-img"/></span>

<h3>Fiverr (DIFM)</h3>
<p></p> <strong>Fiverr, of course, is not a design site exactly.</strong> Its a site where you can hire people from all over the world to do pretty much anything, and that includes a logo design. You can pick the designer you want based on their past work, their prices, the services they offer, and the deadline they promise to meet. Fiverr is one of the more slickly-designed marketplaces overall, and its fairly easy to filter out designers based on your criteria to find one youll like. 
<p></p> They even have a quick and easy wizard to help you get started with the designer-filtering: 
<figure id="attachment_1798541" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1798541"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:80.994803266518% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/features-12.jpg"  width="1347" height="1091" alt="features 12" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/features-12.jpg"   width="1347" height="1091" alt="features 12" class="border wp-image-1798541 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1798541"class="wp-caption-text">Searching for a logo design expert on Fiverr</figcaption></figure> Communicating with the designers youve chosen is fairly easy, although the actual design process will vary a lot. Every designer there works differently, and their process is not dictated to them by the platform. Here are the logos we got:

I personally prefer the type and general design of the first option, but I wish it had the white outline of the second, for contrast. Either way, theyre both adorable. 
<span class="ll-smallimg-wrapper " style="max-width: 776px"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:26.80412371134% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image24.png"  width="776" height="208" alt="Website Planet logo from Fiverr - $40" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image24.png"   width="776" height="208" alt="Website Planet logo from Fiverr - $40" class="border aligncenter wp-image-1008108 ll-img"/></span></span>

<p></p> And lastly, we have the design from the 400-dollar Pro seller, <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=896777&deep_id=0&lang=en&btn_name=NewDirectLinkShortcodeUrl___584555&direct_link=18&amp=0" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink  clickoutLink" target="_blank" onClick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'NewDirectLinkShortcodeUrl___584555', 'fiverrlogodesign', this,  true, );"><strong>animteam</strong></a>. <h3>LogoMaker (DIY)</h3>
<p></p> <strong>LogoMaker is, frankly, not a logo maker that I can recommend.</strong> Its library-based, has a lot of good ideas, but the implementation is flawed, and the whole experience is dated. Worse, pretty much all of the logo designs are quite dated as well, and the logo editor is clunky. This is a service that could be quite good if it got some real updates, but it hasnt had that. 
<figure id="attachment_1798572" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1798572"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:84.879725085911% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/features-13.jpg"  width="1164" height="988" alt="features 13" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/features-13.jpg"   width="1164" height="988" alt="features 13" class="border wp-image-1798572 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1798572"class="wp-caption-text">Examples of LogoMaker logos</figcaption></figure>
<figure id="attachment_1798602" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1798602"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:68.065506653019% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/easeofuse.jpg"  width="977" height="665" alt="easeofuse" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/easeofuse.jpg"   width="977" height="665" alt="easeofuse" class="border wp-image-1798602 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1798602"class="wp-caption-text">LogoMakers editor. Its more annoying to use than it looks</figcaption></figure> The logo I made with this is one of the worst I made during this entire experiment/project. Im sorry. 
<span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:38.6% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/400dpiLogo.jpg"  width="1000" height="386" alt="400dpiLogo" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/400dpiLogo.jpg"   width="1000" height="386" alt="400dpiLogo" class="border aligncenter wp-image-1798631 size-full ll-img"/></span> 
<div class="shortcode-external-button-link"><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=175531&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=ButtonExternalUrl_175531_top10_159_481101&post_id=159&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=top10&amp=0" data-id="175531" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'ButtonExternalUrl_175531_top10_159_481101', 'logomaker', this,  true  );">TRY LOGOMAKER FOR FREE</a></div>
<h3>Looka (DIY)</h3>
<p></p> Looka is an AI-based logo maker that makes fantastic-looking logos. Now, it does use a lot of the same icons that you might find on other services, such as Wix Logo Maker, but it has an edge: beautiful defaults. Theyve done the math, and figured out how to lay out their logos so they look great almost every time. 
<p></p> <strong>The downside to this dedication to aesthetics is that I felt a bit limited in what I could do. </strong>You cant just drag and drop elements around the page. The size and position of your icons and text are managed by sliders, and they have limits. This is all to try to make sure that the user cant accidentally make their logo look too bad. 
<figure id="attachment_1798660" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1798660"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:75.883256528418% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/features-14.jpg"  width="1302" height="988" alt="features 14" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/features-14.jpg"   width="1302" height="988" alt="features 14" class="border wp-image-1798660 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1798660"class="wp-caption-text">Lookas editor</figcaption></figure> This time, the logo I made was, frankly, made to look less like all the other logos. Its not perfect, but its a good example of how even logos with slightly clunky icons can look decent if the layout is spaced out (heh) correctly. 
<span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:29.3% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/31373461_padded_logo.png"  width="1000" height="293" alt="31373461_padded_logo" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/31373461_padded_logo.png"   width="1000" height="293" alt="31373461_padded_logo" class="border aligncenter wp-image-1798690 size-full ll-img"/></span> 
<div class="shortcode-external-button-link"><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=177402&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=ButtonExternalUrl_177402_top10_159_481102&post_id=159&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=top10&amp=0" data-id="177402" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'ButtonExternalUrl_177402_top10_159_481102', 'looka', this,  true  );">TRY LOOKA FOR FREE</a></div>
<h3>Squarespace Logo Maker (DIY)</h3>
<p></p> The Squarespace Logo Maker is an interesting one in that it is completely free. It also doesnt have any premade logos, as such. You get an editor, the ability to add text, and a library of icons from The Noun Project, at least some of which are also used by Looka and Wix Logo Maker. 
<p></p> <strong>The editor is a bit basic, and you cant pick specific sizes for your text or icons. </strong>You have to eyeball everything except the actual layout. Theres a handy grid, and objects sort of snap to each other, so I was able to create a fairly decent, if <em>very</em> basic, logo quickly. 
<figure id="attachment_1798749" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1798749"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:80.048076923077% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/features-15.jpg"  width="1248" height="999" alt="features 15" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/features-15.jpg"   width="1248" height="999" alt="features 15" class="border wp-image-1798749 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1798749"class="wp-caption-text">Designing a logo with Squarespace Logo Maker</figcaption></figure> With my hands tied by the limitations of this editor, I picked an icon that felt a tiny bit less minimalist than the rest, chose a color I liked, and downloaded it. 
<span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:47.52% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/Website-logo-1.png"  width="5000" height="2376" alt="Website logo 1" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/Website-logo-1.png"   width="5000" height="2376" alt="Website logo 1" class="border aligncenter wp-image-1798778 size-full ll-img"/></span> 
<div class="shortcode-external-button-link"><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=975049&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=ButtonExternalUrl_975049_top10_159_481103&post_id=159&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=top10&amp=0" data-id="975049" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'ButtonExternalUrl_975049_top10_159_481103', 'squarespace-logo-maker-review', this,  true  );">MAKE A FREE LOGO ON SQUARESPACE</a></div>
<h3>Tailor Brands (DIY)</h3>
<p></p> <strong>Tailor Brands is AI-based, and they have one of my favorite logo creation processes.</strong> They offer icon-based logos, pure text logos, and logos with randomized abstract shapes. They certainly create some of the more interesting AI-based logos. I just dont particularly like their pricing model, which is a monthly subscription. 
<figure id="attachment_1008398" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1008398"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:74.831460674157% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image3.jpg"  width="1335" height="999" alt="Tailor Brands screenshot - logo editor" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image3.jpg"   width="1335" height="999" alt="Tailor Brands screenshot - logo editor" class="border wp-image-1008398 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1008398"class="wp-caption-text">The Tailor Brands logo editor</figcaption></figure> That is, you only have to pay for one month if you want the logo. Paying for more months gets you some ongoing support, but <em>does not</em> allow you to make further edits to your logo after purchase. 
<p></p> Overall, I enjoyed my experience, and I ended up going with a rather retro logo icon. Its simple, but I think it looks alright, for the price. 
<span class="ll-smallimg-wrapper " style="max-width: 647px"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:24.884080370943% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image23.jpg"  width="647" height="161" alt="Website Planet logo made with Tailor Brands" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image23.jpg"   width="647" height="161" alt="Website Planet logo made with Tailor Brands" class="border aligncenter wp-image-1008427 ll-img"/></span></span> 
<div class="shortcode-external-button-link"><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=63954&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=ButtonExternalUrl_63954_top10_159_481104&post_id=159&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=top10&amp=0" data-id="63954" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'ButtonExternalUrl_63954_top10_159_481104', 'tailor-brands', this,  true  );">TRY TAILOR BRANDS FOR FREE</a></div>
<h3>The Logo Company (DIFM)</h3>
<p></p> <strong>As previously mentioned, The Logo Company works more like a classic design agency.</strong> You provide the brief, someone picks five designers for you, and you get five initial concepts from them. And heres something definitely worth mentioning again: free revisions. 
<p></p> They run all of their projects on Basecamp (its very simple project management software), so they didnt exactly design most of their client experience. Well, at least they didnt design the interface. Even so, everything was made very simple, and they took great pains to explain their entire design process. <strong>They gave me logo concepts, I picked the one I like, and they made revisions until I was happy. That simple.</strong> 
<figure id="attachment_1798807" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1798807"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:100% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/logogrid.jpg"  width="900" height="900" alt="logogrid" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/logogrid.jpg"   width="900" height="900" alt="logogrid" class="border wp-image-1798807 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1798807"class="wp-caption-text">The initial logo concepts</figcaption></figure>
<p style="text-align: left;">Out of all the logo concepts, I liked this one best because it fits our site the best. Its that simple. It looks great at small sizes, the layout is just right, and I particularly liked that bit of sci-fi feel on the type.<br />
<span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:33.7% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/WebsitePD05aR01bP01ZL-Madison1b.png"  width="1000" height="337" alt="WebsitePD05aR01bP01ZL Madison1b" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/WebsitePD05aR01bP01ZL-Madison1b.png"   width="1000" height="337" alt="WebsitePD05aR01bP01ZL Madison1b" class="border aligncenter wp-image-1798836 size-full ll-img"/></span> 
<div class="shortcode-external-button-link"><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=972701&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=ButtonExternalUrl_972701_top10_159_481105&post_id=159&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=top10&amp=0" data-id="972701" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'ButtonExternalUrl_972701_top10_159_481105', 'the-logo-company', this,  true  );">SEE THE LOGO COMPANY&#8217;S LATEST DEALS</a></div>
<h3>Wix Logo Maker (DIY)</h3>
<p></p> Lastly, we have Wix Logo Maker, which (as you might imagine) comes from the people who make the <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/website-builders/wix/" target="_blank" ><strong>Wix website builder</strong></a>. Its got a big library of logos, but theyre not as inspiring as others. Wixs real strength lies in its editor, whichwhile not quite as advanced as DesignEvosis absolutely fantastic. 
<figure id="attachment_1798866" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1798866"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:85.492227979275% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/Wix-Logo-Maker-Is-It-Worth-It-image8.jpg"  width="1158" height="990" alt="Wix Logo Maker Is It Worth It image8" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/Wix-Logo-Maker-Is-It-Worth-It-image8.jpg"   width="1158" height="990" alt="Wix Logo Maker Is It Worth It image8" class="border wp-image-1798866 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1798866"class="wp-caption-text">Wix Logo Maker</figcaption></figure> <strong>If you want to get the most out of Wix Logo Maker, youre going to need to put in some time. </strong>Most of my time mostly went to find an icon that I liked and hadnt used already in one of the other logo makers that share the same library. I rather like how it turned out, even if it could be better. 
<span class="ll-smallimg-wrapper " style="max-width: 609px"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:27.914614121511% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image9.png"  width="609" height="170" alt="Website Planet logo made with Wix Logo Maker" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image9.png"   width="609" height="170" alt="Website Planet logo made with Wix Logo Maker" class="border aligncenter wp-image-1008543 ll-img"/></span></span>

<h3><a id="winner"></a><strong>How Our New Logo Was Chosen</strong></h3>
<p></p> In the end, heres our new logo:<span class="ll-smallimg-wrapper " style="max-width: 670px"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:28.059701492537% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image13.png"  width="670" height="188" alt="Website Planet logo from DesignCrowd" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/image13.png"   width="670" height="188" alt="Website Planet logo from DesignCrowd" class="border aligncenter wp-image-1008079 ll-img"/></span></span> 
<p></p> <strong>A vote was held amongst the Website Planet staff, and it was decided that the logo from DesignCrowd was best. </strong>There was some stiff competition (particularly from the logo from 99designs), but this design won out for a few reasons: 
<ul>
<li>It perfectly fits the Website Planet theme.</li>
<li>It looks great at really small sizes.</li>
<li>As minimalist as it is, it still has personality and a little bit of flair.</li>
<li>I personally love how the type looks fairly straightforward and business-friendly, but has that little bit of sci-fi flair. And yeah, a capital A without the line in the middle is officially sci-fi now.</li>
</ul> Want to know more about DesignCrowd? Read more about my experiences in the <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/logo-design-services/designcrowd/" target="_blank" ><strong>in-depth review</strong></a>. 
<p></p> While DesignCrowd is an excellent option for large businesses and enterprises, it might be overkill for smaller businesses and freelancers who need a great logo, but don&#8217;t want to invest a lot of time and money in it. If that&#8217;s you, I highly recommend you <strong>hop over to Fiverr</strong>to search for the logo designer of your dreams. 
<p></p> With prices starting at only $5, you could even try out a few different designers before you make your final decision &#8211; like holding a little logo design contest of your own. 
<div class="shortcode-external-button-link"><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=896777&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=ButtonExternalUrl_896777_top10_159_481118&post_id=159&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=top10&amp=0" data-id="896777" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'ButtonExternalUrl_896777_top10_159_481118', 'fiverr-logo-design', this,  true  );">FIND A LOGO DESIGNER ON FIVERR</a></div>
<h2 id="hselect-2" class="">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline"> Whats the difference between a logo generator and a logo design service?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">A logo generator is a type of logo design software, accessible through a website or mobile app. Typically, you will have to answer a few short questions about your business. Then, <strong>a variety of logo styles will be generated for you to choose from,</strong> based on the platforms logo design templates. 
<p></p> If you dont have a high budget to invest in your logo or you just like doing things on your own, one of these online logo makers can be an excellent solution for you. If youve never tried your hand at design before, youll be glad to know many platforms provide logo design guidelines. 
<div class="flex flex-grow flex-col gap-3">
<div class="min-h-[20px] flex flex-col items-start gap-4 whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">
<div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert light">
<p></p> A logo design service is a tool that provides various methods to collaborate with expert designers and let them create your logo. Some tools enable you to pick your preferred designer and cooperate with them directly, while others offer you the choice to conduct a logo design competition and select from several alternatives. 
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p></p> Unlike using a logo maker, this logo design process can be lengthy and more complex, but its also the best way to get a unique, custom logo tailored to your needs.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline"> What logo file format do I need? What should be my logos dimensions? And what about logo resolution? </h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline"><strong>It all depends on where youre going to use your logo.</strong> If you only need it for your website or other online use such as social media, a smaller resolution (such as 72dpi) will work great and a PNG logo might be all you need. If you need a transparent logo, youll be glad to know the PNG format supports transparency. 
<p></p> If you have intentions of using your logo in print, a hi-res (300dpi and up) PDF logo could be suitable, but it&#8217;s also wise to have a scalable vector logo format like an SVG logo on hand. This ensures versatility and high-quality reproduction in various scenarios. 
<p></p> If you need an editable file that you or a graphic designer can make changes to later, be sure to get a logo PSD or AI. 
<p></p> As for your logos aspect ratio &#8211; again, it all depends on your plans for your logo. <strong>A square ratio will give you the most flexibility,</strong> while a horizontal logo will still be pretty easy to fit in website headers, social media cover images, and more. A vertical logo might be harder to work with.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline"> When I use one of these services, who owns my logo copyright?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">It depends on the service, but in most cases, <strong>once you purchase a logo, the copyright is yours.</strong> In some cases, you can even file for logo trademark.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline"> Where can I find logo ideas?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Were glad you asked! Logo inspiration is everywhere. Whether you need a new logo or youre planning a logo redesign, keep your eyes open as youre walking down the street or browsing the web. What logos catch your eye? Try to figure out what makes them appeal to you. Is it the icon? The color scheme? The typography? The logo layout? 
<p></p> <strong>Sometimes you can find inspiration in the most unexpected places,</strong> like a birthday card or even a walk through nature. Youll find that some natural shapes are particularly pleasing to the eye, and some typefaces just look right.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline"> How do I choose a color palette for my logo?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Color choices for your logo depend on many things. As color is very subjective, you might want to put your own personal preferences aside and choose a color scheme that reflects your brand identity. 
<p></p> <strong>Ask yourself:</strong> 
<p></p> &#8211; What do I want my brand to reflect and which colors can get that message across? 
<p></p> &#8211; Who is my target audience and what colors would most appeal to them? 
<p></p> &#8211; Where am I going to be using my logo? Will its colors contrast well with different backgrounds? 
<p></p> <strong>Color psychology also plays an important role here.</strong> Dark blues and grays, for instance, evoke a feeling of security, so they can make a good choice for logos with a corporate feel. 
<p></p> Using bright reds and yellows in your logo can truly make it stand out from the crowd. However, it&#8217;s important to exercise caution when employing these colors, as they are also commonly linked with the notion of danger. 
<p></p> Some shades of green, or a combination of greens and blues, will often remind us of nature, while a logo in bright neon green may appear young or even futuristic. 
<p></p> Its always a good idea to familiarize yourself with the color wheel. Complementary colors &#8211; colors on opposite sides of the color wheel, such as red and green or blue and orange &#8211; can create a nice, harmonious color scheme for your logo, with good contrast. Adjacent colors &#8211; colors that are near each other on the wheel, such as red and orange or blue and purple &#8211; can also be a good base for your color palette. 
<span class="ll-smallimg-wrapper " style="max-width: 490px"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:100% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/colour-wheel-1734867_1280.jpg"  width="490" height="490" alt="Color Wheel" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/colour-wheel-1734867_1280.jpg"   width="490" height="490" alt="Color Wheel" class="aligncenter wp-image-1010429 ll-img"/></span></span></span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">  How do I choose my logo font?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Theres no doubt <strong>the font is one of the most important elements of your logo.</strong> Some logos rely on typography alone to get their message across. These are known as logotypes or wordmarks, or even letter logos if they consist of a monogram. 
<p></p> Choose a font that reflects your brand identity. While a serif font can give your logo a classic, trustworthy look, sleek sans-serif fonts can look more contemporary. 
<p></p> Its always a good idea to keep things simple. Stick with a clear, crisp font that is easily readable even at smaller sizes. Avoid overly decorative fonts, as they can come across as tacky. 
<p></p> A mix of too many fonts is never a good thing, but if you have a logo tagline, you might want to make it in a different font that complements the main font. 
<p></p> <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/best-free-fonts/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><strong>Don&#8217;t miss our list of the top 70+ free fonts.</strong></a></span> 
</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
